There's no water component to this, so you need to add the moisture to your skin yourself before sealing it in with the butters and oils in this cream. That's the first rule of natural skincare that I've learned- never put oils or butters on dry skin, because they won't soak in properly, plusthey don't provide moisture on their own. I believe that's the problem a lot of people are having when they say this is greasy or doesn't sink in. Hope that helps someone!
